\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02134}02134\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{such\ as\ \`{}tuple[int,\ str]\`{}\ or\ a\ \`{}TypeVarTuple\`{},\ and\ 'pulls\ them\ out'.\ For}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02235}02235\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02236}02236\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ In\ the\ same\ way\ that\ a\ normal\ type\ variable\ is\ a\ stand-\/in\ for\ a\ single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02237}02237\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ type\ such\ as\ \`{}\`{}int\`{}\`{},\ a\ type\ variable\ *tuple*\ is\ a\ stand-\/in\ for\ a\ *tuple*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02238}02238\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ type\ such\ as\ \`{}\`{}Tuple[int,\ str]\`{}\`{}.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02240}02240\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Type\ variable\ tuples\ can\ be\ used\ in\ \`{}\`{}Generic\`{}\`{}\ declarations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02241}02241\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Consider\ the\ following\ example::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02242}02242\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02243}02243\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ class\ Array(Generic[*Ts]):\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02244}02244\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02245}02245\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ \`{}\`{}Ts\`{}\`{}\ type\ variable\ tuple\ here\ behaves\ like\ \`{}\`{}tuple[T1,\ T2]\`{}\`{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02246}02246\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ where\ \`{}\`{}T1\`{}\`{}\ and\ \`{}\`{}T2\`{}\`{}\ are\ type\ variables.\ To\ use\ these\ type\ variables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02247}02247\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ as\ type\ parameters\ of\ \`{}\`{}Array\`{}\`{},\ we\ must\ *unpack*\ the\ type\ variable\ tuple\ using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02248}02248\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ star\ operator:\ \`{}\`{}*Ts\`{}\`{}.\ The\ signature\ of\ \`{}\`{}Array\`{}\`{}\ then\ behaves}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02249}02249\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ as\ if\ we\ had\ simply\ written\ \`{}\`{}class\ Array(Generic[T1,\ T2]):\ ...\`{}\`{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02250}02250\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ In\ contrast\ to\ \`{}\`{}Generic[T1,\ T2]\`{}\`{},\ however,\ \`{}\`{}Generic[*Shape]\`{}\`{}\ allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02251}02251\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ us\ to\ parameterise\ the\ class\ with\ an\ *arbitrary*\ number\ of\ type\ parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02252}02252\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
